constraint KLUDGE_MATERIALS_TO_KB {
	objects:
		?KR is_a (300)VARONIS
	condition:
		?KR.IS_MATERIAL_INSTANCE = 'NA'
	restrictions:
		find_or_create ((material)(300) (nr=DUMMY_MATERIAL))
	explanations:
		"This constraint given to us within Steve G's Passive Receiving Creation Steps Summary"
}
